*Intel job# **744223 =E2=80=94 Logic Technology Development Reliability Eng=
ineer*=20
<http://www.intel.com/content/www/us/en/jobs/job-search/rcg2.html?job=3D719=
752&src=3DUNV-10180>
=20=20

*Job Description*: You will define roadmaps to meet requirements, goals and=
=20
milestones for a new technology process. Defines and establishes flow,=20
procedures, and equipment configuration for the module. Selects and=20
develops material and equipment for the process to meet quality,=20
reliability, cost, yield, productivity and manufacture requirements. Plans=
=20
and conducts experiments to fully characterize the process throughout the=
=20
development cycle. Drives improvements on quality, reliability, cost,=20
yield, process stability/capability, productivity and safety/ergonomic over=
=20
variables such as material, method, equipment, environment and operating=20
personnel. Develops solutions to problems utilizing formal education,=20
statistical knowledge, and problem-solving tools. Establishes process=20
control systems for the process module and sustains the module through=20
volume ramp. Develops strategy to resolve difficult problems and=20
establishes systems to deal with these problems in the future. Trains=20
production/receiving process engineers for transfer to other factories.=20
Transfers process to high volume manufacturing and provide support in new=
=20
factory start-up as well as install and qualification of the new production=
=20
lines.=20

=20

*Your responsibilities may include but not be limited to:*

-Designing and executing experiments to determine the necessary parameters=
=20
for reliability model development and validation.=20

-Developing new acceleration techniques and analytical tools to assure the=
=20
early identification of potential reliability problems with new products,=
=20
packaging, boards, and manufacturing processes.=20

-Developing risk assessments and making quality and reliability predictions=
=20
based on data that you will collect using statistical principles and design=
=20
of experiments fundamentals=20

-Evaluating materials, properties and techniques used in production from a=
=20
reliability standpoint.=20

-Creating reliability design layout rules and specifications.=20

-Advising design engineering on selection, application and test of=20
electronic components and systems.=20

-Collaboration with cross functional teams to solve technical / reliability=
=20
issues during technology development and ramp to high-volume manufacturing.=
=20

-Recommending process technology certification evaluation and acceptance=20
criteria.=20

-Recommending material, design or test methods and statistical process=20
control procedures for achieving required levels of product reliability.=20

-Partners may include Logic Technology Development (LTD), wafer Fab=20
Manufacturing and Test (FSM), Assembly & Test Technology Development=20
(ATTD), Assembly and Test Manufacturing (ATM), Intel Custom Foundry (ICF),=
=20
and partners within Intel's Customer Quality Network (CQN) focused on=20
Product, Development, and Manufacturing Reliability.

=20

=20=20

*Qualifications:*

=20

*For 744223, Logic Technology Development Reliability Engineer: *

This is an entry level position for a technical college graduate with a=20
Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering, Material Science, Physics or=20
related discipline.=20

*Preferred Qualifications:*

-Experience in experimental design, execution, and interpretation.=20

-Experience with electron device fabrication and characterization.=20

-Experience with electrical measurement equipment in characterizing=20
electron devices (e.g. HP4155, oscilloscope, etc.)=20

-Experience with a range of analytical techniques such as SIMS, EEL, EDX,=
=20
XPS, Auger, acoustic profiling, FTIR, AFM, etc.=20

-Experience with various lab imaging techniques (SEM, FIB, TEM, etc.)=20

-Knowledge in one or more of the following areas electron device=20
fabrication, semiconductor device physics, CMOS transistor level circuit=20
design, interconnect reliability, soft error rate and circuit simulations,=
=20
PCB fabrication principles, surface mount assembly, board test methods,=20
solder and laminate material behavior under mechanical or thermo-mechanical=
=20
conditions.=20

-Knowledge of semiconductor wafer fabrication process and process=20
integration challenges.=20

-Knowledge of silicon and packaging assembly integration, or PCB technology=
=20
operations=20

-Understanding of reliability failure statistics, physics, or failure=20
mechanisms.=20

-Experience programming with formal language (C,C++, C#, etc.) and=20
scripting language (AWK, PERL, Python, SQL, TCL, VBScript, etc.)=20

-Experience with sequel or SQL data extraction.=20

-Experience with statistical analysis packages (e.g. SAS, JMP, Minitab, R,=
=20
etc.)=20

-Prior Intel Intern or Scholarship recipient

=20

*Logic Technology Development Reliability *consists of transistor,=20
interconnect, far-back-end, ESD/LU, and test chip design, D1D ramp, and D1C=
=20
ramp groups. Groups are located at the Ronler Acres campus and embedded=20
into Logic Technology Development teams.

=20

*For 739889,  Logic Technology Development Reliability Intern:*

=20

*Job Description: *Responsibilities may consist of measurement data=20
acquisition and analysis of electron devices, building device level models,=
=20
or other types of data analysis related to transistor, interconnect, defect=
=20
reliability, Si-package interaction, or soft error rate development=20
efforts. Intern will be responsible for data collection, analysis, model=20
formulation, and communicating results based on a 3 month summer project.=
=20

=20

*Qualifications:*

*Required:*  This is an entry level position for a college graduate student=
=20
working towards a Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering, Materials=20
Science, Physics or related discipline

*Preferred:*  Experience or academic background in some areas as listed=20
above for permanent opening.
